padding-bottom: 0.372em;">r</span></span><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.151em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">e</span></span><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.151em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">e</span></span><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.151em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">n</span></span><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.151em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">e</span></span><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">d</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 0.006<span id="S4.p13.m8" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\pm"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">±</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>0.111 mag. The value is still positive albeit with a large error. This means that in this statistically more uncertain differential consideration <span id="S4.p13.m9" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1/3 cannot be ruled out at this <span id="S4.p13.m10" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> value. On the other hand, <span id="S4.p13.m11" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1 can be ruled out to 92%. For <span id="S4.p13.m12" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 10<span id="S4.p13.m13" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-6}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">6</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> a meaningful differential determination is not possible, because only the value for one galaxy is available for the screened sample.</p>
</div>
<div id="S4.p14" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Very obviously, increasing the number of shielded and unscreened galaxies with measured FGLR distances would make the result more significant. At this point, our results support the conclusions found by <cite class="ltx_cite ltx_citemacro_citet">Jain<span class="ltx_text ltx_bib_etal"> et al.</span> (<a href="#bib.bib176" title="Astrophysical Tests of Modified Gravity: Constraints from Distance Indicators in the Nearby Universe" class="ltx_ref">2013</a>)</cite> as described in section 3.</p>
</div>
</section>
<section id="S5" class="ltx_section">
<h2 class="ltx_title ltx_title_section">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_section">5 </span>Summary and conclusions</h2>

<div id="S5.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">We have constructed stellar evolution models for massive stars in the range from 12 <span id="S5.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="M_{\odot}\;"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base" style="margin-right: -0.081em;"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.446em; padding-bottom: 0.298em; padding-right: 0.081em;">M</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">⊙</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mjx-mspace" style="width: 0.278em; height: 0px;"></span></span></span></span></span></span>&nbsp;to 60 <span id="S5.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="M_{\odot}\;"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base" style="margin-right: -0.081em;"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.446em; padding-bottom: 0.298em; padding-right: 0.081em;">M</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">⊙</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mjx-mspace" style="width: 0.278em; height: 0px;"></span></span></span></span></span></span>&nbsp;accounting for the influence of modified gravity in the equation of hydrostatic equilibrium. We find an increase of stellar luminosity already on the main sequence and the effect becomes stronger in the BSG phase. The reason is the change in internal density stratification. BSG with their contracted core and strongly expanded envelope have a core-halo density structure, which leaves a large fraction of the stellar volume unscreened against a potential fifth force. In consequence, clear effects of modified gravity are encountered for the evolutionary tracks in the HRD and sHRD.</p>
</div>
<div id="S5.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Using the evolutionary tracks in the BSG phase we can construct a theoretical FGLR diagram, where we display <span id="S5.p2.m1" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="M_{\mathrm{bol}}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base" style="margin-right: -0.081em;"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.446em; padding-bottom: 0.298em; padding-right: 0.081em;">M</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.219em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">b</span></span><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.151em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">o</span></span><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">l</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>&nbsp;against <span id="S5.p2.m2" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\log g_{F}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">log</span></span><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char"></span></span><span class="mjx-msubsup MJXc-space1"><span class="mjx-base" style="margin-right: -0.003em;"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em; padding-right: 0.003em;">g</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.446em; padding-bottom: 0.298em; padding-right: 0.106em;">F</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. The comparison with observations in the LMC reveals an offset between the observed and theoretical FGLRs which was already noted in previous work and which may be caused by deficiencies of the spectral diagnostics leading to the observed FGLR or uncertainties of the stellar evolution treatment leading to BSG. However, the differential effects between the stellar evolution calculations with Newtonian gravity and modified gravity still allow for an estimate of the influence of modified gravity on FGLR distance determinations. Distance moduli would become 0.15 mag larger for a fifth force parameter <span id="S5.p2.m3" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1 and shielding parameters <span id="S5.p2.m4" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 5<span id="S5.p2.m5" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\times"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">×</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>10<span id="S5.p2.m6" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-7}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">7</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and 10<span id="S5.p2.m7" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-6}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">6</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. We use a comparison between observed TRGB distances, which should be unaffected by modified gravity, and FGLR distances in galaxies shielded and unscreened against the fifth force to constrain <span id="S5.p2.m8" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>. If we assume that there is no systematic offset between TRGB and FGLR distances, then we find that <span id="S5.p2.m9" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1 can be ruled out with 96% confidence. For <span id="S5.p2.m10" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1/3 modified gravity distance moduli would increase by 0.05 mag and 0.075 mag for <span id="S5.p2.m11" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 5<span id="S5.p2.m12" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\times"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">×</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>10<span id="S5.p2.m13" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-7}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">7</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and 10<span id="S5.p2.m14" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-6}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">6</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, respectively. The constraints on modified gravity are slightly weaker in this case. <span id="S5.p2.m15" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 5<span id="S5.p2.m16" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\times"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">×</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>10<span id="S5.p2.m17" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-7}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">7</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is unlikely by 89% and <span id="S5.p2.m18" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 10<span id="S5.p2.m19" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-6}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">6</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> by 95%. If we allow for a potential systematic offset between TRGB and FGLR distances, then the constraining results are more uncertain. For <span id="S5.p2.m20" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 5<span id="S5.p2.m21" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\times"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">×</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>10<span id="S5.p2.m22" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-7}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">7</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> <span id="S5.p2.m23" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1 can still be ruled out to 92% but <span id="S5.p2.m24" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1/3 is unlikely only to 60%. For <span id="S5.p2.m25" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 10<span id="S5.p2.m26" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-6}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">6</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> no constraints are possible, because the sample of shielded galaxies is too small. In summary, the results are comparable with the ones obtained by <cite class="ltx_cite ltx_citemacro_citet">Jain<span class="ltx_text ltx_bib_etal"> et al.</span> (<a href="#bib.bib176" title="Astrophysical Tests of Modified Gravity: Constraints from Distance Indicators in the Nearby Universe" class="ltx_ref">2013</a>)</cite> from a study of Cepheid stars, where for <span id="S5.p2.m27" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1/3 values of <span id="S5.p2.m28" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}\geqq"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.519em;">χ</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mjx-mo MJXc-space3"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-ams-R" style="padding-top: 0.519em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">≧</span></span></span></span></span></span></span> 5<span id="S5.p2.m29" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\times"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">×</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>10<span id="S5.p2.m30" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="{}^{-7}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-texatom"><span class="mjx-mrow"></span></span></span><span class="mjx-sup" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em; padding-bottom: 0.446em;">−</span></span><span class="mjx-mn"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.372em; padding-bottom: 0.372em;">7</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> were be ruled out with 95% confidence and for <span id="S5.p2.m31" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\alpha_{c}"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">α</span></span></span><span class="mjx-sub" style="font-size: 70.7%; vertical-align: -0.212em; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; padding-bottom: 0.298em;">c</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = 1 values of <span id="S5.p2.m32" class="ltx_Math"><span class="mjpage"><span class="mjx-chtml"><span class="mjx-math" aria-label="\chi_{c}\geqq"><span class="mjx-mrow" aria-hidden="true"><span class="mjx-msubsup"><span class="mjx-base"><span class="mjx-mi"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-math-I" style="padding-top: 0.225em; vertical-align: 0.513em; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0.071em;"><span class="mjx-texatom" style=""><span class="mjx-mrow"><span class="mjx-mo"><span class="mjx-char MJXc-TeX-main-R" style="padding-top: 0.298em;
